country_event = { #peace out responce
	id = newyork_prewar.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: newyork_prewar.8"}
	title = newyork_prewar.8.t
	desc = newyork_prewar.8.d
	picture = GFX_ACW_american_brigade

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #yes
		name = newyork_prewar.8.a
		clr_country_flag = NYC_can_invade_america
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 357 #Maine
					state = 934 #New Hampshire
					state = 933 #Vermont
					state = 932 #Massachusetts
					state = 935 #Rhode Island
					state = 931 #Connecticut
					state = 796 #Upstate New York
					state = 359 #New Jersey
				}
			}
			NYC = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { controls_state = 360 }
			NYC = {
				transfer_state = 360
				add_state_core = 360
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { controls_state = 1162 }
			NYC = {
				transfer_state = 1162
				add_state_core = 1162
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = ALA
						tag = COR
						tag = CSA
						tag = USA
						tag = TEX
						tag = WCC
						tag = CAL
					}
				}
				white_peace = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = newyork_prewar.10
				days = 15
			}
		}

		
	}
}

country_event = { #sexy oraange NEE or nah 
	id = newyork_prewar.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: newyork_prewar.8"}
	title = newyork_prewar.10.t
	desc = newyork_prewar.10.d
	picture = GFX_ACW_american_brigade

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #yes
		name = newyork_prewar.10.a
		add_political_power = 50
	}
	option = { #yes
		name = newyork_prewar.10.b
		if = {
		limit = {
		NOT = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = NYC_harlem_mob
		has_cosmetic_tag = NYC_harlem
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NYC_NEE
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = NYC_harlem_mob
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NYC_NEE_harlem_mob
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = NYC_harlem
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NYC_NEE_harlem
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = NYC_harlem_socialist
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NYC_NEE_harlem_socialist
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = newengland.2009
				days = 15
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = national_populist
				}
				country_event = {
					id = NYC_flavor.276
					days = 23
				}
			}
		}
		
	}
}

			}

		}

					state = 932 #Massachusetts

				days = 5
			}
			country_event = {
				id = NYC_flavor.101
				days = 22
			}
		}
	}
	title = NYC.156.t
	desc = NYC.156.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NYC_newyork_1

	trigger = {
		tag = NYC
		owns_state = 361 #Maryland
		owns_state = 371 #Louisiana
		owns_state = 395 #Illinois
		owns_state = 797 #San Francisco
		owns_state = 932 #Massachusetts
		NOT = {
			country_exists = TEX
			country_exists = CSA
			country_exists = USA
			country_exists = CAL
			OR = {
				has_government = syndicalist
				has_country_flag = NYC_harlem_nationalists
				has_country_leader = { name = "Casper Holstein" ruling_only = yes }
				has_country_leader = { name = "Stephanie St. Clair" ruling_only = yes }
				has_country_leader = { name = "Bumpy Johnson" ruling_only = yes }
			}
		}
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #yay
		name = NYC.156.a
		add_political_power = 10
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = USA
					is_core_of = CSA
					is_core_of = COR
					is_core_of = TEX
					is_core_of = WCC
					is_core_of = CAL
				}
			}
			NYC = { add_state_core = PREV }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Lewis J. Valentine"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = NYC_flavor.96
					days = 40
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
					has_government = totalist
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NYC_USA_FDR
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
					has_government = national_populist
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = NYC_USA
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = radical_socialist }
			country_event = NYC.157
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			country_event = NYC.158
		}
		else = { country_event = NYC.159 }
	}
}

	id = NYC_flavor.9
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: NYC_flavor.1"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Fred Trump" ruling_only = yes }
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			country_event = {	
				id = NYC_flavor.90
				days = 40
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = totalist
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Franklin D. Roosevelt Jr."
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			country_event = {	
				id = NYC_flavor.653
				days = 40
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = radical_socialist }
			country_event = {	
				id = NYC_flavor.91
				days = 40
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			country_event = {	
				id = NYC_flavor.92
				days = 40
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
			country_event = {	
				id = NYC_flavor.93
				days = 40
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = national_populist }
			country_event = {	
				id = NYC_flavor.292
				days = 40
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
			country_event = {	
				id = NYC_flavor.94
				days = 40
			}
		}
	}
	title = NYC_flavor.9.t
	desc = NYC_flavor.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NYC_statue_of_liberty

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = NYC_flavor.9.a
		set_capital = { state = 361 }
		add_political_power = -25
		
	}
	option = { #
		name = NYC_flavor.9.b
		add_political_power = 75
		
	}
	
}

				name = "Fulgencio Batista"

			}

			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = "The Corporation"
				name = "The Corporation"
			}
			hidden_effect = { 
                set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.5 }
				remove_all_ministers = yes 
			}
			add_ideas = {
				CUB_Joe_Stassi_hog_pau
